Attacked by the Left and Right Wings, the Spanish Cabinet Resigns En Masse 26

The Republican System is in a Precarious State

The Catholic Agrarian Party Holds the Key to the Overall Situation

The Socialist Party Has a Conspiracy to Launch a Major Uprising

Madrid The Spanish government was laughed to death today. Afterwards, the leader of the Catholics rose to speak, and his criticism of the government was extremely激昂. So the Prime Minister asked other minority parties to express their opinions, but none responded. The government then adjourned to consider its position, and then announced its resignation. (1st Reuters News Agency)

Madrid The turbulent political situation in Spain has prompted the resignation of the Samper cabinet, plunging the republican system into a precarious state. Since the discovery of a conspiracy by the Socialist Party and the Communist Party to launch an uprising in September, the country has been in a state of alert. Now, it must either fully accept the provisions of the Constitution, or submit to the demands of the Socialist Party, the Industrial Revolution Party, and the Communist Party to immediately implement the labor dictatorship. The key to the overall situation is in the hands of the Catholic Agrarian Party. Its leader, Robles, has always been behind the scenes in mixed cabinets, and now he is using the situation to demand power from President Zamora. President is in this situation, but has to take extreme action to dissolve Congress. This is his second and last dissolution of Congress, because according to the Constitution, the President can only dissolve Congress twice during his term of office. Although the Socialist Party has the appearance of a major uprising, the President seems to be planning to have Lerroux, the leader of the Radical Party, organize a majority party government and invite the Catholic Agrarian Party to participate. Now he is waiting for a reply from Robles, who holds fascist views, to determine his course of action. Robles is tired of the rule of minority parties, or for the sake of gaining dictatorial power, he may change his entry into the Republican Party. Then many Catholics will abandon him, the imperialists will withdraw all their support, and the Socialist Party will be most saddened. Now it is rumored that if this move is realized, they will definitely stab the middle class in the chest.

According to reports, on September 19, the authorities detained a student and found a plan for a labor revolution in his arms, which planned to start by burning government offices and slaughtering those wearing uniforms. On the same day, a convertible car was found in the university city, full of military equipment and ammunition, proving that the anti-Catholic alliance was plotting to join hands with the revolutionary Socialist Party. Previously, a week ago, it was rumored that the Socialist Party was preparing a large number of military equipment and ammunition. Later, two Socialist Party congressmen were found at a certain seashore monitoring the transportation of 73 boxes of ammunition. On September 20, the government issued a notice to reassure the people, saying that there was no danger of revolution at present, but most of the people did not believe it, because they knew that several government offices had narrowly escaped being bombed, so they thought that the Socialist Party would sooner or later provoke a war. (2nd Reuters News Agency)

Madrid The Spanish cabinet resigned late last night because Robles, the leader of the right wing of the Acción Popular Party, attacked the cabinet's agricultural reform and Catalan autonomy policies in Congress. The general public admitted this morning that Prime Minister Samper's resignation was a serious problem facing President Zamora. The attack on the government in Congress was a sign that the Acción Popular Party believed that the time had come for the party to directly participate in politics. It is found that the party is the largest political party of minority parties in Congress. Now, if the cabinet resigns as approved by the President, or will organize a center-right majority party government, the Acción Popular Party will be able to gain one or two cabinet seats, but its leader is afraid that he will not be able to participate in person. Samper and his cabinet members had long known that the waves were about to rise and were overthrown by Congress, so some cabinet members advocated resigning first to avoid debate in Congress. The Acción Popular Party and the Radical Party cannot cooperate, so it is generally believed that it is difficult for the party and the Radical Party to form a cabinet together. It is not yet known whether the President is willing to trust a majority government, because after the establishment of a majority cabinet, it will cause a violent opposition from the left wing, and Lerroux, the leader of the Radical Party, recently expressed satisfaction with the Samper government, but Lerroux is also afraid that Samper will not be able to win in Congress, so it is better to have Samper resign early. The Radical Party may try to have Lerroux form a cabinet, but if the time is not yet ripe, it is also possible for Samper to reorganize the cabinet. The current problem must be decided by the President. If a center-right majority party government is organized, the Socialist Party and the left-wing Republican Party will withdraw from Congress, and a very difficult political situation will occur. (2nd National News Agency)

It is now reported that the Prime Minister sent a long telegram to the Foreign Minister to persuade him to stay, and King Carol also spoke with the Foreign Minister on the phone. However, it is said that the Foreign Minister is determined to resign and does not want to do it again. (National Telegram, 2nd)

(Geneva) – Regarding the Romanian cabinet reshuffle, according to the local Havas News Agency representative, the initial resignation was actually by Foreign Minister Titulescu. He had repeatedly expressed his desire to be the leader of Romania's foreign policy and bear all responsibilities, but he always encountered resistance and was therefore discouraged. (Havas Telegram, 1st)

Bucharest – The Romanian cabinet officially resigned today because Minister of Industry and Commerce Teodorescu resigned. The cabinet must be completely reorganized. It is likely that Prime Minister Tătărescu will change several cabinet members and then immediately resume his duties. (National Telegram, 1st)

Former Prime Minister Ordered to Form a New Cabinet 31

Titulescu Refuses to Participate

Prime Minister to Concurrently Serve as Foreign Minister

Capital of Romania – After the cabinet tendered its resignation, the King still entrusted former Prime Minister Tătărescu to continue forming the cabinet. Tătărescu has gone to Sinaia to present the list of the new cabinet to the King. The members of the second Tătărescu cabinet are not much different from the members of his first cabinet, except that Foreign Minister Titulescu will resign. Although the government is extremely silent about Titulescu's attitude, political figures generally believe that Titulescu refuses to participate in the new cabinet and is very determined, and there is no way to reverse it. The new cabinet will appoint Sterian as Minister of Industry and Commerce, Prime Minister Tătărescu concurrently serves as Acting Foreign Minister, and De Juvara serves as Deputy Foreign Minister. It is reported that Free Party leader Brătianu has expressed his agreement with Tătărescu's new cabinet. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

Sudden Political Upheaval Has Two Reasons 32

Capital of Romania – Various "message newspapers" without political colors discuss the cabinet's resignation and are surprised that the political upheaval happened so suddenly. The opinions of the newspapers all believe that there are two political upheavals this time, one is the political upheaval within the Free Party, and the other is the political upheaval about Titulescu. Their severity is equal to each other, and they think that the new cabinet will be difficult to exist without Titulescu's participation. As for Prime Minister Tătărescu's intentions, the newspapers believe that he will retain some old cabinet members, and the rest will be sought from the Free Party's young members. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

Conflicting Opinions Within the Cabinet on Foreign Policy 33

Capital of Romania – Regarding the resignation of the Tătărescu cabinet, it is said that Foreign Minister Titulescu caused disagreement due to foreign policy issues, which must be verified. Titulescu had already resigned before the entire cabinet submitted its resignation, but the cabinet's resignation was definitely not affected by Titulescu's resignation. It is heard that the reason why Titulescu resigned was because of disagreements with Prime Minister Tătărescu on the issue of minorities being discussed in Geneva. Tătărescu is still optimistic and will meet with the King tonight to discuss the political situation. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

France Loses a Friend: Signs of a Separation Between Romania and France 34

(Paris) – The Paris Echo and other French newspapers all attach great importance to the political upheaval in Romania, and they say that the resignation of Foreign Minister Titulescu was caused by relations with Germany. This is because Titulescu is recognized as the cornerstone of France's Central European and Balkan policies. Now that this cornerstone has collapsed, France feels a sense of shared adversity. The Paris Echo reported that Titulescu's resignation is causing peace-loving people to feel uneasy in this eventful time. The L'Action reported that Polish Foreign Minister Beck's bold actions in Geneva on the issue of minorities were the trigger for the Romanian cabinet upheaval. The Journal reported that the Romanian cabinet upheaval was caused by France's pro-Russian policy, and that the resignation of Foreign Minister Titulescu is the key to the separation between France and Romania. France has lost Romania after Poland. (National Telegram, 2nd)

(Paris) – The newspapers here unanimously expressed regret over the resignation of the Romanian cabinet, because Titulescu loves peace and is a friend of France. The newspapers all believe that the resignation of the Romanian cabinet was caused by foreign policy issues, especially some incidents in Geneva, and they want to hope that Titulescu will return to office soon. "L'Echosi Avoir" said, "The opinions of the member states of the League of Nations Council on the amendment of the clauses related to the rights of minorities in the Treaty of Versailles seem to be directly or indirectly related to the Romanian political upheaval." The Journal said, "The facts that happened in Geneva did not meet Titulescu's expectations, and the Soviet Union's entry into the League also reduced the effectiveness of the alliance between Poland and Romania. Titulescu's resignation may be an attempt to clarify the domestic political situation with a slam on the table, and it is not intentional to resign." The Paris Echo said, "Titulescu has made great contributions to Romania, but why does the Romanian authorities seem to not know how to be grateful to Titulescu? The answer to this question should be sought in two things: one is the political suspicion, and the other is the pressure exerted by Berlin, Rome, and Warsaw on Romania's internal affairs." The L'Ere Nouvelle reported that Titulescu strongly advocates getting close to the Soviet Union. Titulescu is the only one in Romania who advocates this policy, and he bravely advocates it. The newspaper also said that the enemies of the Little Entente are all happy to see Titulescu's departure. (Havas Telegram, 2nd)

Roosevelt's Speech Disappoints the American Banking Community 35

Labor Unions are Very Pleased

(New York) – Wall Street, the financial center of the country, almost unanimously expressed disappointment with President Roosevelt's broadcast speech last night that the government is still determined to control industry and commerce, and they believe it is purely a political act. The President did not mention whether the dollar could be stabilized or whether the budget could be balanced, and they believed that this was a major mistake in this speech. A well-known broker said, "The business community hoped that the President would guarantee mutually linked efforts for recovery, but the President, like Washington's attitude recently, attacked Wall Street and the banking community." The banking community was even more indignant that the President said that they could not assist the government as the British banking community did. However, other aspects of the President's attitude toward private capital and labor-management relations were supported. Newspaper rhetoric was inconsistent. The labor side, according to the announcement of the annual meeting of the San Francisco General Labor Union, was very pleased. The president of the union, Green, said that the President's speech showed that the government was determined to maintain labor's right to collective bargaining, which would be enough to promote labor-management relations. (National Telegram, 1st)

(Washington) – It is unanimously recognized here that industry and commerce will support President Roosevelt's industrial truce plan, and it is hoped that a 30-hour work week will be established. The labor side believes that the President's speech is a sign that the government supports collective bargaining. The National Association of Manufacturers said that the President was asked to maintain the status quo during the truce period, and that labor unions should give up strikes as a means of unity. The president of the American Federation of Labor, Green, replied to the National Association of Manufacturers that the association's suggestion was just a disguise, but said that the 30-hour work week was the only practical way to relieve unemployment. (National Telegram, 1st)

(Washington) – Director of the Reconstruction Administration, General Johnson, tearfully left political life today, and said goodbye to the staff of the Reconstruction Administration in tears. International Commercial Telegram

October 2nd Reuters Special Commercial Telegram 73

Gold and Silver 74

London Gold Price: Today's gold price is 142 shillings, 2.25 pence, up 8.5 pence.

London Silver Bar: London silver price rose 1.875 today. Spot price is 22.625 pence, and futures price is 22.75 pence. India and speculators bought in, while China sold, but not much. The market closed steady.

Bombay Silver Bar: Bombay silver price, spot price is 62 rupees, up 6 annas. November futures 62 rupees 1 anna, December futures 62 rupees 3 annas, each up 7 annas.

Exchange Rates 75

British-American: The London foreign exchange market opened chaotically and only calmed down at noon due to intervention from official circles. However, an uncertain trend emerged again in the afternoon. The opening exchange rate for British-American was $4.975, one cent lower than yesterday's closing rate. At 11:00, it rose 1.375 cents to $4.92125. At noon, it fell 0.375 cents. At 1:00 PM, it fell another 23/32 of a cent to $4.9171875. At 2:00 PM, it rose 3/32 of a cent to $4.92125.

British-French: The opening exchange rate was 74.03 francs, 25 points lower than yesterday's price. At 11:00, it rose 18 points to 74.21 francs. In the afternoon, it fell another 6 points to 74.15 francs. The market began to calm down at 1:00 PM in the afternoon, but at 2:00 PM, it rose another 13 points to 74.28 francs.

American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market, the opening exchange rate for American-British this morning was $4.92, 0.25 higher than yesterday's close. It then rose another 0.25 to $4.9225. This is the most recent price.

Cotton and Wheat 76

New York Cotton: The cotton market opened down 6 to 8 points due to profit-taking by longs and short selling. Sentiment is still steady. At 10:20, the price rose 5 points, but foreign interest in the cotton market was weak, so the price fell 3 points. However, the most recent prices have risen 4 points and fallen 1 point.

Liverpool Wheat: Wheat fell sharply this morning. At 1:00 PM, the December futures were 5 shillings, 3.375 pence, down 1.75 pence.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market also fell. At 1:00 PM, the January futures price was 6.57, down 6 points.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market fell today due to profit-taking by longs. Although brokers and European exporters bought in later, the market still closed lower. The price of April-May futures for Biloch cotton was 308 rupees, down 1 rupee.

Chicago Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened lower by 0.75 to 1 point due to profit-taking by longs. However, the most recent prices have risen 0.25 because someone bought in when the price fell.

Rubber 77

London: The rubber market initially showed sympathy with the US market situation and turned loose, but then remained stable. At noon, the traded price for January-March futures was 7.1875 pence, down 0.1875 pence.

New York: Rubber opened up 8 to 9 points. At 10:40, buying resumed, and the price rose another 5 to 6 points compared to the opening.

Factors unfavorable to the market situation were: (1) although market conditions are low, there are not many buyers, and goods are weak, especially cotton; (2) the exchange rate trend is chaotic, causing market conditions to be uncertain. Recent News of Bandit Suppression in Southern Jiangxi 80

Daily Necessities Cut Off from Bandit Areas

Food and Salt Especially Scarce

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Communist bandits in southern Jiangxi have recently concentrated in Huichang and Xingguo, showing signs of plotting a southward escape. According to a recent report from the front lines: (1) On the 20th of the month, based on intelligence, over a hundred bandits, labeled a "pseudo-independent regiment," were harassing areas such as Yetian. A battalion was immediately dispatched to encircle and suppress them, and the bandits, unable to withstand the attack, fled into the mountains. Over thirty bandits were killed, five male and female bandits were captured, nine firearms, five hand grenades, two boxes of gunpowder, and a bandit banner were seized. (2) The troops stationed in Anyuan recently dispatched a team to search and suppress the remaining Communists in the vicinity. In the Bantian area near Tianxinxu, they encountered several hundred Communist bandits and engaged in a fierce battle. After the government troops launched a fierce counterattack, over a hundred bandits were killed and a pseudo-company commander was captured. (3) In Chang'anbu Huangnipaidi in Xinfeng County, the Communist bandit Pseudo-Guerrilla Brigade Commander Lan Guanglian, hiding in Zhuwu, colluded with criminals, anesthetized ignorant farmers, and induced them to become bandits. Our army learned of this and immediately went to encircle and suppress them, capturing the pseudo-brigade commander on the spot, as well as Chen Kunxian, a pseudo-Soviet land commissioner and special agent. Many hand grenades and pseudo-official documents and propaganda items were seized. (4) Huang Heling, who came to Gan County from Maodian on the 23rd, stated that when he escaped from the bandit lair, the bandit area was scarred and devastated, with only old women and children to be seen, and very few strong men. Food was scarce, and daily necessities were cut off, with salt and kerosene being the most lacking. (September 28th)

Heavy Rain in Xuzhou, River Waters Rise Sharply 81

City Streets Three Feet Deep in Water

Various Rivers Show Signs of Flooding

Xuzhou Correspondence: Since the Yellow River was diverted during the late Qing Dynasty, although river disasters have been eliminated, water conservancy has been neglected, river channels have become silted up, and tributaries have been blocked. Even the ditches and canals in the fields have not been dredged. Droughts result in thousands of miles of barren land, while floods result in overflowing waters. Xubu is surrounded by the old course of the Yellow River on three sides, and the terrain is like the bottom of a pot, causing the bed of the old Yellow River to be tens of feet higher than the city. In recent years, whenever there is continuous rain, the people of Xubu fear the disasters, and the farmland in the countryside is even more disregarded. This year, in the spring, the Tong County government ordered the districts to dredge the rivers, slightly clearing the waterways, and heavy rains in the summer did not cause a disaster. However, the low-lying city of Xubu and the construction funds for dredging Wenqu Ditch have been delayed time and again by the Construction Department, causing delays in effectiveness. Whenever there is heavy rain, the city residents are always on alert. However, now that the summer season has passed, suddenly there was heavy rain for days, (29th, 30th). The rain on the night of the 29th was especially heavy. City streets turned into rivers in an instant, with rainfall of over three feet on flat ground. The amount of water in the old Yellow River at the northeast two passes suddenly increased, reaching the bridge holes. The Kui River, which needs to be closed, had water level with the banks. The water depth in the northwest corner of the city, behind the county government, and in the southeast corner, inside the park, reached the knees, and most of the streets and alleys were blocked by water. Fortunately, the main hub of Quwen Ditch had been repaired locally, and the water has receded today. However, the water in the Huhhe River attached to the city has continued to increase. This is because the area affected by this heavy rain is very wide, and most of Xuzhou Prefecture has been affected. The Wei Lake and lower irrigation rivers in northern Xuzhou, the Zhong Canal in eastern Xuzhou, the Kui River in southern Xuzhou, the Longdai River in Xiaoxian County, and the Dasha River in Fengpei County have all flooded. Fortunately, the Lanfeng Dike has not yet collapsed, which is a slight consolation to the people. However, this hinders the sowing of winter wheat and affects the coming spring, so it seems that preparations must be made in advance. It has been noted that the water conservancy of Xubu was previously proposed by the Third Army Commander Wang Jun to use military engineers to build the road outside the New East Gate and to reorganize the old dikes of the Yellow River around the city to prevent floods. The administrative meeting of the Tongshan County Government also resolved to dredge the old course of the Yellow River in the northeast two passes, down to Jizuiba, to create a large and small reservoir, and to separately divert the water from the Bajian Spring in the southwest Hanwang Township eastwards into Shitou Lake, returning abandoned fields to the lake, in order to facilitate storage and discharge. These three projects are the fundamental issues of Xubu water conservancy. (1st)

National Army Captures Yongxing, a Key Border Area 82

Upstream and Downstream Are Key Routes for Assaulting Bandit Capital

Troops Occupy After Multiple Assaults

Nanchang Correspondence: The upstream and downstream areas on the border of Yongfeng and Xingguo are characterized by towering mountains and rugged terrain, making them a key route for the bandit suppression army to directly attack the bandit capital, Ruijin. They have long been occupied by the Communist bandits. On September 25th, troops were ordered to attack the area. The bandits, relying on their defensible position, put up a stubborn resistance. The troops advanced bravely, launching several assaults, and finally defeated the bandits. The bandit ranks suffered heavy casualties. The troops definitively occupied the area that afternoon. The opposing bandits were the entire pseudo-23rd Division and the pseudo-21st Division, among others. (September 29th)

Yangtze River National Goods Tour 83

(2) Heng

We set off from Shanghai, dividing into land and water routes. I took the land route. Upon arriving in Nanjing, transportation became a problem. Later, I found a transfer company with Bian cars (light motor vehicles) directly to Wuhu. Because there were limited seats, I was sitting next to the driver. Our deputy head, Chen Weizhong, was sitting on the roof of the car. The road along the way was very flat. At Huangshan Ferry on the Anhui border, there were boats to carry the Bian car across the river, entering Taiping County. Farmers along the highway were already harvesting rice, which was gratifying and uplifting. Sitting in the car, I couldn't help but feel a sense of longing, thinking that water conservancy and road construction are all constructions related to the people's livelihood. Like Nanjing to Wuhu, it originally took more than a day to travel, but now it can be reached in three hours. We cannot but praise the merits of road construction.

After arriving in Wuhu, I visited administrative agencies, the press, and industry associations, all of whom agreed to support us. We borrowed the YMCA as a venue and began preparations. Because the venue had already been borrowed on the 30th, we had to postpone the opening to the 31st. Because we had ample time, we decided to go to neighboring counties to do publicity work. I was responsible for going to Xuan City. Xuan City was called Ningguo Prefecture in the Qing Dynasty and held a high position in Anhui. There is a saying, "South Xuan and North Hefei." North Hefei refers to Hefei in northern Anhui. Now the Zhawu Railway (from Zhaoxian to Wuhu) has reached Xuan City. I took the train and saw that the railway management was very clean, but there were very few passengers. The car body vibrated and tilted, the reason being that the roadbed was uneven. But I in the car not only did not feel disgusted, but felt happy. The small stations along the way are mostly made of wooden boards, and the platforms are made of wooden posts covered with mud, which is very economical. The number of bridges is no less than that of the Huhang Railway (Shanghai-Hangzhou), which shows the hard work of the people involved. There are more than 100,000 residents in Xuan City. There are cross streets. The folk customs are simple. Many silk and cloth shops also sell foreign and Guangdong goods. Meiya silk sells very well. Zhonghua Enamel and Sanxing toothpaste are also selling well. Most of the cigarettes are domestic products. Levers' Soap has penetrated the area. Ren Dan (a medicine) is openly sold. Business in the shops is bleak, which has never happened before. This year's rice harvest is not good, and the commerce is feared to have no hope.

On the evening of the 31st, the opening ceremony of the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory's domestic silk exhibition was held. More than one hundred people attended, including administrative officials, the 78th Division Commander Fu, and guests from all walks of life. They all expressed keen hope for Meiya's promotion of domestic goods. From September 1st to the 5th, there were five days of meetings, two fashion shows, and two screenings of the Meiya self-produced film "Chinese Silk." The audience was very excited and considered it an unprecedented event in Wuhu. A total of more than 27,000 people visited, with women accounting for three-fifths, which is slightly less than three-tenths of the entire population of Wuhu. At the same time, major silk and cloth shops held a grand sale of Meiya silk, and buyers were crowded every day. The goods they brought were sold out. As a result of this event, the people of Wuhu have a deeper understanding of domestic goods, especially for women. (To be continued)

The American Overseas Chinese Cultural Advancement Association Established in Beijing 84

Chen Lifu Attends and Delivers an Admonitory Speech

Beijing News: Huang Wenshan, Wang Qi, and others initiated the American Overseas Chinese Cultural Advancement Association in Beijing. After submitting an application to the Central Party Headquarters and receiving a license, they actively prepared for the establishment. On the morning of the 30th of last month, at 8:00 AM, the founding meeting was held at Minghuchun, Xinjiekou, the capital city. Dozens of members and more than ten representatives attended, and the ceremony was solemn. The chairman, Wang Qi, announced the reasons for the meeting, and Huang Wenshan reported on the preparations. Then, Chen Lifu, director of the Organization Department of the Central Party Headquarters, gave a speech, which was full of warnings and encouragements. Next, Jin Zimao, instructor of the People's Movement Committee of the Central Party Headquarters, and Shi Lianfang, representative of the Ministry of Interior, gave speeches. Wang Zhiyuan, representative of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee, and Jian Jianghan and Wei Shisheng, members of the association, followed with speeches. Then, officers were elected. As a result of the ballot, Huang Wenshan, Wang Qi, Meng Guangzhao, Tang Jihe, Jian Jianghan, Qu Zhaoqing, Huang Biying, Chen Huabai, and Huang Gongjue were elected as directors. He Ruocang, Ren Wuwei, and Wu Xiangjun were elected as alternate directors. Finally, a tea party was held, and the meeting adjourned.

Songjiang 85

Training Instructor of the Defense Corps Defrauds Money

Jiang Ruiwen, a graduate of the training center of the former county defense corps, is young, amorous, and does not engage in proper work. His life is becoming increasingly impoverished. Recently, he suddenly came up with the idea of defrauding money from various places. Yesterday, he went to the Wang family at No. 12 Guangming Bridge Alley to sell sound recordings for two yuan and one dime per two. The Wang woman thought the price was cheap, so she gave him four yuan and two dimes to buy two two's worth. Unexpectedly, Jiang left and never returned. Knowing that something was wrong, someone found him at the Luoshen Temple station and dragged him to the Wang's house. Jiang, knowing that defrauding money was against the law, secretly held a knife and attempted to stab Li Shijun, the younger brother of Wang Li. Fortunately, he was unsuccessful and escaped disaster. He was taken to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau for mutual accusations. The Public Security Bureau is now sending personnel to investigate in order to resolve the matter.

Changshu 86

All Tax Collectors Arrested and Imprisoned

The county has accumulated a large amount of unpaid land taxes over the years. The provincial departments have repeatedly urged payment, but it has not been cleared. The eastern township of the Sixth District is the worst in the entire county. The county government recently discovered that this unpaid tax was due to the negligence of the tax collectors, or even their arbitrary embezzlement. Therefore, the officials were ordered to strictly pursue the payment. Unexpectedly, eleven tax collectors from the district, including Gao Fengqian, submitted a petition requesting a temporary postponement of the collection. On the afternoon of the 1st, they jointly went to the county government to personally deliver it. The head of the Second Section, Tang Chengsi, relayed in the reception room, saying that you tax collectors are the ones who urge grain from the landowners. Now you are submitting an absurd petition to avoid collection. What is your intention? The people cannot request this kind of accumulated debt, etc. At that time, each official initially agreed to pay in installments, but then there was no specific number, so the police immediately ordered the arrest and imprisonment of all officials.

Suzhou 87

Frequent Reports of Robberies in the Countryside

In recent times, robberies and kidnappings have been heard of in the villages and towns of Wu County, especially in Hengjing and other towns along Taihu Lake. Villagers are really experiencing sleepless nights. Unexpectedly, news came that the Zhou family in Zhouxi, Xishan Township, was robbed again on the night of the 1st, with a loss of more than 500 gold. There was also a robbery in Hugengshang, Zhouzhuang Township, but the loss was small. The Second District Detective Team of the Water Public Security Bureau captured the robbers yesterday at Xuezhedun.

There is a rumor that the security team, which was formed by the merger and transformation of the Wu County Defense Corps and the Police Team, is being investigated and trained under orders. Therefore, Chairman Shi of the Wu County Chamber of Commerce, due to the frequent reports of robberies in the four rural areas of Wu County, specifically discussed the matter with the Wu County Magistrate, requesting that they be exempted from being transferred to the province for training in order to maintain local peace and order. The Wu County Magistrate immediately reported to the province for approval. It is now heard that approval has been granted. The Wu County Magistrate also issued a notice to various townships yesterday (2nd), strictly guarding against the lake bandits' restless movements.

The County Anti-Smoking Association Investigates and Arrests Smokers 88

Since the Wu County Anti-Smoking Association implemented compulsory registration of smokers, it has already ended. A total of more than 16,000 people have registered in the entire county. The association started its investigation work yesterday (2nd). It is heard that the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association will send an inspection team to Suzhou in the next few days, which will search house to house. If any smokers have not registered, they will be arrested and punished. Those with serious circumstances will be shot on the spot. All soil ointment shops in the county will be established on the 5th and begin operating.

Wuxi 89

Gambling Arrest in Ganlu Town

Conflict Between Land and Water Police

Gao Shichun, the director of the Seventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau in Dangkou Town, District 8, sent Police Chief Lin Langqiu and twelve policemen to Zhongxing Tea House and Yuexi Inn in Ganlu Town nearby at more than 3 pm yesterday to arrest eight gamblers. Afterwards, four young women who were gambling were arrested in the Wang family's house and taken together to the lookout post of the Seventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau in Ganlu Town. Unexpectedly, over forty members of the first squad of the ninth team of the second district of the water police, who were stationed in the town, went to the lookout post and pleaded with Police Chief Lin, saying that two of the arrested young women were relatives and requesting their release. Police Chief Lin refused, which led to a conflict and a tense situation. Five policemen, including Wu Ruixing, Sun Yaotang, and Li Shaohua, were slightly injured. Later, through mediation by local people, Chief Gao and Team Leader Chen of the Water Police also did not want the situation to escalate, and they immediately resolved it peacefully. The arrested gamblers were also fined and the case was closed.

Suicide at a Shanghai Youth Hostel 90

Cen Zhitang (字天祥), a 24-year-old son of the owner of Jisheng Pharmacy on Route Braine in Shanghai, was from Yuyao, Zhejiang. His father, named Jishi, in his fifties, was a well-reputed doctor practicing in Shanghai. Zhitang was currently working at the Shanghai Municipal Council handling housing tax matters, earning a substantial income. He married his cousin, Yu Meiqin, at the age of twenty, and they had a daughter in the first month of this year. However, Shanghai being a den of iniquity, Zhitang inevitably spent lavishly, which his father disapproved of and severely reprimanded him for. In a fit of pique, Zhitang conceived the idea of suicide and left home on the 26th of last month. He arrived in Wuxi on the evening of the 28th and stayed in room 103 on the third floor of the New World Hotel. On the evening of the 30th, he swallowed two bottles of "Middina" and one bottle of "Adalin" and lay down covered with a blanket. The next day at noon, the hotel's tea server, Shi Maorong, noticed that the guest had not yet gotten up and did not respond to calls. Suspecting something was amiss, he reported to the front desk. They climbed into the room through the balcony and found him pale and delirious, clearly poisoned. He was immediately sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but due to the severity of the poisoning, rescue was impossible. He died at 4 PM. Before taking the poison, Zhitang wrote two suicide notes, one to his brother Cen Peng, and one to his wife, Meiqin. Yesterday (the 2nd), the deceased's family received the news and came to Wuxi, accompanied by the local village head, Xi Zhiliang, to report to the county court's prosecutor's office, requesting exemption from an autopsy.

Changzhou 91

A Farmer Watching Rice Paddy Killed by Cutting

Chen Xikun, a farmer from Hanshu Village in the Fourth District of Wuba, went to the fields to watch over his rice paddy at approximately 7 PM on the 30th of last month. He agreed with his wife, née Xu, that they would take turns guarding the fields after dinner. When his wife went as agreed at around 8 PM, she could not find her husband. She searched everywhere and called out his name, but there was no response. She went home to get a lamp and returned to search. She caught sight of her husband lying on the ground, with cuts on his head and shoulders. He had already died. Chen Xu was greatly alarmed, and cried over his body. She immediately went to the nearby police station to report the murder. Patrol officer Xu Xing immediately went to investigate the scene and discovered bloodstains on the head of Chen Gengrong, a villager from the same village. The stains were clearly visible and appeared to be related to the case. He was brought to the station for preliminary interrogation, but his statements were evasive. Yesterday (October 1st), a document was prepared to request the county court to send personnel for an autopsy, and Chen Gengrong was detained for further investigation.

Jiangyin 92

Accident Involving a Wuxi-Jiangyin Long-Distance Bus

Yesterday (30th) at around 4 PM, the Wuxi-Jiangyin long-distance bus, car number 29, was traveling from Jiangyin to Wuxi. When passing the south end of Qingyang Station, it struck a farmer named Zhao Aqit, injuring his head, right foot, and left shoulder. He was bleeding heavily and lost consciousness. The Qingyang substation ordered the original vehicle to transport him to the city and sent him to Jiangyin Hospital for treatment, fearing for his life.

Nantong 93

Urban Land Valuation Completed

Nantong has completed the city land price declaration, starting with land surveying. The assistance committee considered the local prosperity and estimated land prices, dividing them into ten grades, with the highest at 1,000 yuan per mu and the lowest at 100 yuan. Farmland in the city was estimated at 40 yuan per mu.

Yangzhou 94

A Case of Manufacturing Pills Discovered in Daqiao Township

The Daqiao Public Security Seventh Sub-station received a report that the Wang Zhang family in Wangjiazhuang, northeast of the town, was manufacturing red pills. Police officers were dispatched to search and found two boards used for making red pills and small sieves. They were brought to the station for preliminary interrogation. It was stated that the items were stored there by Qi Youyu in April. The Wang Zhang family had a daughter-in-law, née Fu, who had worked as a wet nurse for the Qi family, and thus they were acquainted. According to the statement, Officer Zheng arrested Qi Youyu and, along with Wang Zhang and the evidence, transferred them to the bureau yesterday to be sent to the county for disposal.

Difficulty in Establishing Yangzhou-Huoshan Automobile Service 95

The Yangzhou-Huoshan road in Jiangdu County was originally used by the privately operated Xingyang Automobile Company. Later, Tang Shaoxuan, a businessman from Yiling, submitted a request to raise capital and operate the Yangzhou-Huoshan automobile service on that road. The county bureau reported this to the Construction Department, which instructed the county to ban Xingyang Automobile Company, which had not yet registered, and instructed the county to transfer the matter to the bureau and convene the businessmen for discussions on a joint public-private operation. Unexpectedly, the businessman even claimed that the previous submission was a false claim and requested a name change. He also stated that raising funds for the Yangzhou-Huoshan automobile service was not easy and requested an extension or to solicit other merchants to rush the matter. The submission was reported to the county. The county bureau now considered that the businessman had submitted a request to undertake the Yangzhou-Huoshan automobile service and then a request to cancel it. Now, he was requesting corrections, which was absurd. Yesterday (the 1st), in addition to the county bureau jointly issuing a reprimand, it also reported to the Construction Department for instructions in order to comply with the order.

Hangzhou 96

Zhejiang Autumn Cocoon Harvest of 40,000 Dan

Since the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department borrowed 3 million yuan from the Shanghai banking community to control the purchase of autumn cocoons, due to the abundant yield, since the opening of weighing on the 20th of last month, 15,400 dan of fresh cocoons have been collected, reeled into 450 to 600 jin. It is estimated that more than 20,000 dan can be collected continuously. In addition to spending one million yuan from the Bank of China for cocoon funds, another 500,000 yuan will be spent successively to meet the needs. The Construction Department specially held a meeting yesterday to decide that the cocoon collection matters would end on the 20th of this month and decided to merge the Silk Reeling Committee into the Cocoon Collection Committee to be responsible for handling cocoon collection and silk reeling matters. Xia Daoxiang, a sericulture expert from the Ministry of Industry, has come to Hangzhou to preside over the improvement of silk reeling.

Jiashan 97

Disaster Victims from Various Places Flock to Beg for Food

Outside the West Gate of this county, disaster victims from Tongxiang, Chongde, Shimenwan, Tudian Temple, Jiaxing, and other places have arrived in droves, supporting the old and carrying the young, begging for food along the way. Their condition is pitiful. When begging for food, they all describe the disaster situation, and tears accompany their voices. Today, they are visible everywhere in the streets and alleys of the city, especially white-haired old women, begging door to door. It is said that these disaster victims all came from Zhenze, Jiangsu, suffered severely from drought, and were unable to survive, drifting to this place.

Large Gang of Female Bandits Rampaging in the Northern Countryside 98

In the area bordering Qingpu and this county, a large gang of female bandits has recently been discovered, numbering over a hundred, with sharp firearms and a fierce momentum. Their chieftain, named Wang Meimei, is from Shanyang, Songjiang. They have repeatedly looted property and seized weapons in the Zhangliantang area. Recently, they have gathered in the towns and villages of Qingliang'an, Fanbang, and Yaozhuang Bridge in this county, ready to cause trouble. The residents of that area are greatly alarmed and are moving away in droves. After receiving the news, the Seventh Water Police Team stationed in Xitang ordered a strong force to go to suppress them in separate groups.

Letter

Letter from the Xiang-E Section Administration Bureau of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway 99

Having recently read in your newspaper of September 18th the report titled "Xiang-E Train Derails, Hankou Telegram of the 17th, the Xiang-E Railway's 103rd Additional Train, which departed Ezhou for Xiangzhou on the 15th, derailed near Yuezhou, overturning eight cars, injuring five disaster victims and two passengers, the 5th express train was blocked, and traffic was not restored until the 16th," I was greatly surprised. After investigating, there was no derailment or injury to passengers on this line. Furthermore, there was no 103rd additional train. I think that this is a misreport. I am writing to you to request that you investigate and correct the report to avoid confusion and to ensure the accuracy of the news. Sincerely, Chief of the Bureau, Yin Deyang, September 28th.

Local News

This Year's Double Tenth National Day 100

The National Crisis Persists, No Foreign Guests Will Be Invited

Central News Agency: October 10th is the National Day of our country. In the past, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs routinely invited foreign guests to celebrate. Last year, due to the severe national crisis, in addition to the ambassadors and ministers of various countries in China automatically going to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to offer congratulations, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs did not formally invite foreign guests to celebrate. Now, time has passed, and it is another year. The national crisis is as severe as before. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs specifically instructed the Shanghai Office yesterday to notify the ambassadors and ministers of various countries staying in Shanghai that this year's Double Tenth Festival will still follow last year's practice of abolishing the invitation of foreign guests to celebrate.

Robert Bredon, Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, issued a notice yesterday, informing merchants that the office will be closed for one day on October 10th, the Double Tenth National Day.

Eurasia's Giant Aircraft Flew to Lanzhou Yesterday Morning 101

Carrying Gan Naikang and Others to Beijing

Preparing to Extend the Lanzhou-Baotou Section of the Air Route

Shenshi News Agency: Eurasia Aviation Corporation's Junkers Ju 52 giant aircraft officially took off from Shanghai Hongqiao Airport at 9 AM yesterday morning to join the Shanghai-Xinjiang route for its first test flight. According to the Shenshi News Agency reporter's inquiry with the company, this flight was piloted by Otto Tezsos, the Hansa Company pilot who came with the aircraft, with telegraph operator Hensgen and mechanic Kurtshoff assisting. Also traveling with them were Meng Tiefu, the Eurasia Company's flight director. Upon stopping in Beijing, it landed at Ming Palace Airport, carrying Gan Naikang, Zhang Daofan, Li Dijun, Director of the Information Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Li Jingcong, the company's general manager who had recently come to Beijing. They took off for Shaanxi and Gansu at 10 AM. The company sent Meng Tiefu to Lanzhou to conduct on-site inspections in order to extend the Lanzhou-Ningxia line to Baotou. Meng will return to Shanghai on the original aircraft to report. In the future, after the Lanzhou-Ningxia line is extended to Baotou, this aircraft may still fly on this route. However, Baotou has not yet been test-flown, and it is still questionable whether an air station can be established there. The use of giant aircraft on this line is not fixed and will depend on the company's profitability on each line and the number of passengers. As for Xinjiang, there has been no response since the company sent a telegram. The Shanghai-Dihua section will take some time to restore.

Cotton and Rice in the County Suffer from Wind and Rain Again, Causing Mildew 102

The cotton and rice in various districts of Shanghai County suffered from drought this summer. After receiving the report, the county government immediately sent Tao Lan and others to various districts to investigate. They returned to the county and reported that the overall harvest in the county was determined to be eight-tenths, and the case was reported to the provincial government for dispatching personnel to re-survey the area. Now, the county government has received a report from Xi Langqing, director of the county agricultural association, stating that since the beginning of autumn, there have been continuous winds and rains, and most of the cotton and rice have become moldy, making the autumn harvest hopeless, which is very different from the previous survey. He requested that personnel be sent again to re-survey the area and that relief be provided to maintain poor farmers. In addition to sending the original committee members to re-survey and verify the situation, the county government has also sent telegrams to the provincial government and the Ministries of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Construction, urging them to send personnel to the county for joint survey immediately.

India Needs Our Country's Products 103

Please Contact the Guidance Department of the Trade Bureau for Introduction

The International Trade Bureau is doing its best to introduce domestic products for export in order to develop foreign trade. However, it is not responsible for delivery, payment, transportation, and other matters. These matters are to be directly negotiated by the importers and exporters. An Indian importer and exporter wants to purchase domestic products, and the details are as follows:

Straw Mats, Fans, and Firecrackers 104

Straw mats, fans, and firecrackers are special products of our country. The number exported abroad every year is quite large. They are not only welcomed by overseas Chinese, but also by foreigners. Recently, the Karachi Hua Lai Import and Export Company in Mumbai, India, needs these goods. Manufacturers can write to the bureau for introduction.

Fennel Oil and Cinnamon Oil 105

Fennel oil, Turpentine oil, and Clove oil are produced in Guangdong and Guangxi and are the main ingredients for spices. They are also essential raw materials for soap, cosmetics, and the brewing industry. In addition, they have a wide range of uses in medicine. The value of exports to European and American countries every year is very large. The Ship brand is the most famous for these spices in foreign markets. The Mohan Xin Import and Export Company in India needs the above-mentioned fragrant oils. Those who are engaged in this business can write to the guidance department of the bureau for introduction.

After the Promulgation of the Jiangsu Provincial Public Debt Regulations, Negotiate Mortgage Cash 106

Zhao Dihua Negotiates with Shanghai Banking Circles

The Public Debt Is Issued at 98% of Face Value

Xinxin News Agency: The Jiangsu Provincial Government has presented to the Central Government for approval the issuance of 20 million yuan of public debt for water conservancy construction and industrial promotion. The regulations for this public debt have been promulgated by order of the National Government. The provincial government is currently soliciting bids for printing, and is also negotiating with banking circles for mortgage cash. The details are as follows:

Soliciting Bids for Printing 107

The Jiangsu Provincial Government Finance Department stated that the public debt regulations have been passed by the 179th meeting of the Executive Yuan, ratified by the Legislative Yuan, and promulgated by order of the National Government on the 1st. In order to issue the debt as soon as possible, it is now soliciting bids for printing. The public debt tickets are divided into four types: 10,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan, all in unregistered form. It is expected that it will take one or two months to complete the printing of all the tickets. Therefore, the actual date of official issuance has not yet been determined.

Issuance at 98% 108

The use of this public debt has been decided to be entirely for construction projects, and the distribution of uses is as follows: (1) 14 million for the first phase of the Jiangsu Reclamation Area water conservancy project, labor recruitment, dredging, and guiding the Huai River into the sea; (2) 4 million for drought relief and industrial promotion; (3) 2 million for consolidating a portion of the debt, totaling 20 million yuan. In the future, it will be issued at 98% of face value, with an annual interest rate of 6%. The Jiangsu Province tobacco and alcohol license tax, the stove tax allocated to Jiangsu Province by the Ministry of Finance, and the field and house deed tax of each county in Jiangsu Province are designated as the principal and interest repayment fund. If it is not enough, it will be supplemented from the field tax. The principal will be repaid by lottery twice a year in March and September, and the principal and interest will be fully repaid in thirteen years.

Negotiate Mortgage 109

Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Department, and Shen Baixian, Director of the Construction Department, believe that the construction of water conservancy and the promotion of industry and other matters urgently need to be carried out. They have negotiated with Shanghai banking circles to mortgage the public debt for cash to be used for these purposes. It is reported that the banking circles have expressed approval for the mortgage. After further negotiations, it should be realized. It has not yet been decided whether to mortgage all or part of the debt.

Uniform Adoption of the New System for Public Weights and Measures 113

Ministry of Railways Instructs Two Railways to Comply

The two railway administrations received instructions from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, stating: "The Executive Yuan instructed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce presented a report stating that the National Bureau of Weights and Measures reported that the First National Weights and Measures Promotion Committee resolved that the national public weights and measures should be unified by the end of the 19th year. The former Ministry of Industry and Commerce presented this to the Executive Yuan, which forwarded it to the National Government for record and distributed it to the central ministries, commissions, and provincial and municipal governments, instructing their subordinates to take note of the case. Now, the civil weights and measures in various provinces and cities have gradually been unified. However, many government agencies that use weights and measures for public purposes have completely complied with the new system, while others are still using the old system or the British system, which is affecting the promotion and urgently needs to be promoted to complete the task. How should this be handled? Please review and instruct. Based on this, this case has been overdue for a long time and has not been thoroughly completed, which has greatly affected the prospects of unification. In view of the above, in addition to instructions, it is appropriate to prepare a document requesting your review and approval, and requesting you to instruct the central ministries, commissions, and provincial and municipal governments to instruct their subordinate agencies to uniformly adopt the new system within the shortest possible time if they have not yet done so, in order to emphasize the importance of laws and orders. Based on this, in addition to issuing orders and requesting the National Government to instruct its directly affiliated agencies to comply, it is appropriate to order you to comply with the above. This order."

Sharp Decline in Japanese Goods Imports in September 114

According to yesterday's Japanese-language Mainichi Shimbun, the import of Japanese goods into this port had been increasing since the revision of tariffs in July. Therefore, the prospects for trade with China were optimistic. However, the situation suddenly became sluggish in September. According to the handling of the Japan Mail Shipping Line, the association currently has no detailed statistics to publish, but the overall amount is less than 20,000 tons, which is a decrease of more than 5,000 tons compared to August. The reason for this is that bulk sugar has been overwhelmed by Javanese products, and the Kansai region has suffered from wind and water damage, so the import of groceries and other goods has almost stopped since the end of September. However, seafood imported from Hokkaido is still active and is expected to increase in the future. However, the general purchasing power is gradually declining. As for the goods from the Kansai region, it may not be possible to recover in a short period of time because the grocery manufacturing factories in that area have been greatly affected by wind and water damage. Therefore, the prospects for the import of Japanese goods into this port are worrying.

Food Grain Surplus Leads to Falling Rice Prices 125

More than one yuan cheaper than a month ago.

Limited sales of foreign rice lead to stockpiling.

New Rice Arrives in Shanghai 126

New early rice from Wuxi, Changzhou, Jiangyin, Suzhou, Tongli, Jiaxing, Fengjing, Pinghu, Xindai, and other places, after being milled and polished, is sold to rice merchants inland. After being whitened by inland merchants, it is loaded onto barges and transported to Shanghai. Approximately forty boats arrive daily at the rice industry docks in both the northern and southern parts of the city. The largest barges can carry up to 500 piculs, while the smallest can carry over 100 piculs. Averaging 250 piculs per boat, approximately 10,000 piculs of new rice arrive in Shanghai daily.

Stockpiling of Old Rice 127

A reporter from the Ta Kung News Agency conducted a survey yesterday of rice shops, rice mills, grain shops, and rice retailers (the rice inventory of small rice shops of a retail nature was not counted) in the city’s rice market. The amount of old rice stockpiled reached 300,000 piculs. Due to the stockpiling of old rice and the large quantities of new rice arriving in Shanghai, the price of rice in the Shanghai market is declining daily. Yesterday's rice price lists issued by the market showed that the highest price was 12.10 yuan to 12.50 yuan, which is more than one yuan cheaper compared to a month ago. No. 2 rice, such as Tongli white broken rice, was 11 yuan, and rice from Sijing, Fengjing, and Xindai was 10.10 to 10.20 yuan. No. 3 rice, such as Lujian, Muchen, Pingwang, Qingling, Shengchuan, and Xitang, had fallen to around 9.70 yuan and 8.70 yuan. The reason for this price drop is the surplus of both new and old rice, coupled with a large stock of foreign rice.

Sluggish Sales of Foreign Rice 128

Shanghai rice merchants have ordered over one million bags of Saigon rice from British firms such as Tyler and Darfur, including near-term shipments for September and October, and far-term shipments for March of the twenty-fourth year, along with orders from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi provinces. Of this, 500,000 bags have already been shipped to China. Over 100,000 bags of the September-October term rice have arrived in Shanghai. The rest are being shipped directly to the provinces by the managing foreign firms. Because new domestic rice is entering the market everywhere and there is a particularly large stockpile of old rice in Shanghai, transactions of Saigon rice by various merchant guilds are limited. The recent Saigon rice imported by rice merchants is being affected by sluggish sales, and the combined interest on loans since March means that no profit can be made.

Page 11

Magistrate Ye Fenghu of Hang County Comes to Shanghai to Beg for Aid 129

Drought in Zhejiang Province, coinciding with rural bankruptcy, has caused the people's livelihood to become even more difficult. Hang County, the premier county of Zhejiang, has been affected by recession for many years, leading to the decline of commerce and trade, and social economy is even more strained. This drought has lasted for three months, rivers have dried up, crops have withered, and the autumn harvest is completely hopeless. The local authorities have done everything in their power to prevent and rescue the situation, but ultimately, without a drop of water from above or a trickle from below, they could not save even a fraction of the situation. In addition, the autumn silkworm harvest has been poor, and all kinds of industries that farmers rely on for their livelihoods have completely given up hope. It is estimated that the drought will cause losses of more than seven million yuan. As the time for the recent autumn harvest approached, farmers lay prostrate in the fields, weeping and wailing, or in groups to go to the county to petition. And in the villages, there are tragedies of wives selling their children, and starving Hang County disaster victims crying out for food.

Suicides are also heard from time to time. If no relief is provided, hundreds of thousands of mournful cries will all starve to death. Therefore, County Magistrate Ye Fenghu gathered people from the party and government organs, local impartial gentry, and formed a drought prevention and disaster relief association to concentrate efforts on raising funds for relief. However, due to the wide disaster area and the large number of disaster victims, it is not easy to raise funds locally. County Magistrate Ye Fenghu, accompanied by Police Chief Chen Chunbai, and local gentry Zhong Weishi, Wang Jianqing, and Wu Zihou, traveled to Shanghai to seek aid from Zhejiang gentry in Shanghai and various charitable organizations in Shanghai, and brought with them a relief plan, giving a detailed account of the drought relief plan. The day before yesterday, he went to the Red Cross and the All-Zhejiang Association to request aid. Yesterday, he attended the A-Xu Disaster Relief Association meeting to report on the disaster situation. The gentlemen present were very moved and expressed their intention to do everything possible to provide relief to benefit the victims.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Asks the Finance Bureau to Improve Tax Regulations on Brokers 130

To be handled in accordance with the joint meeting of various industries.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Finance Bureau yesterday, stating, "Since the promulgation of the broker registration tax in this city, which is handled by the municipal government, various broker trade associations have sent letters, all claiming that the complexity of the grading system, the restrictions on commissions, and the severity of the penalties are unbearable for the brokers. They have requested a meeting to seek relief measures, etc. On September 27, representatives from the Bean and Rice Trade, Timber Trade, Seafood and Grocery Trade, Fruit and Produce Trade, Pig Trade, Flower Trade, Liang Shaojiu Trade, Chicken and Duck Trade, and Produce Trade associations were convened to hold a joint meeting, and the following resolutions were made on the spot: (1) Please postpone the implementation. (Reason) The Broker Business Regulations were originally scheduled to be implemented on October 1, but the time is too urgent and should be postponed. (2) Commissions should be handled according to the industry regulations approved by the Social Bureau. (Reason) See Article 18 of the Broker Business Regulations. (3) The commodity grading system is copied from the regulations set by Jiangsu Province and is not applicable to Shanghai. It should be formulated based on the actual situation in Shanghai and taking into account the opinions of various industries. (Reason) For example, the Bean and Rice Trade alone is divided into as many as twelve categories: Rice Trade, Rice Trade, Lu Chen Trade, Grain Trade, Bean Trade, Oil Trade, Peanut Trade, Cake Trade, Grain Measure Trade, Cottonseed Trade, Melon Seed Trade, and Bran Trade. For example, the Fruit and Produce Trade is divided into as many as eight categories: Fruit Trade, Peanut Trade, Melon Trade, Water Chestnut and Lotus Root Trade, Vegetable Trade, Bamboo Shoot Trade, Radish Trade, and Yam Trade. (4) Registration certificates must be certified and collected by the trade associations. (5) If tax invoices from previous years are lost during tax collection, no penalties should be imposed. (6) Photo attachment should be waived when obtaining licenses, etc." These were recorded on file. Now that the implementation period is near, since the industry members have stated various obstacles, improvement measures should be given to facilitate implementation. We hereby send this letter, hoping that your bureau will examine and approve the adoption of the resolutions made at the industry joint meeting, to promote public friendship.

Shanghai County's Handling of the Anti-Smoking Campaign Since April 131

Smokers account for 1.3% of the total population.

Establishment of a smoking cessation center with an attached clinic.

The Shanghai County Government established the County Anti-Smoking Committee on June 1st of this year, as ordered by the provincial government, to handle the anti-smoking campaign within a limited time. In addition to organizing the articles of association according to the provincial order, County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia and Police Chief Xu Yubin also appointed Zhang Jingye, Standing Committee Member of the County Party Department, Huang Yunzhen, Director of the County Production Office, and Yao Huiquan as appointed committee members. On May 23rd, the County Anti-Smoking Committee was established in advance. Internally, it was divided into four sections according to regulations: General Affairs, Investigation and Arrest, Licensing, and Auditing. First, various articles and regulations promulgated by the province were extracted and printed in a special booklet. Together with the Party Department and its affiliated self-government, education, and public security organs, anti-smoking propaganda meetings were held in various districts to investigate and inform people of the laws, explain the advantages and disadvantages, and encourage smokers to be self-aware. Later, the county public security bureaus, district township offices, and social education organs were supervised to conduct a survey of smokers throughout the county and to register smokers. At the same time, in accordance with the Provincial Regulations on the Prohibition of Opium Shops, merchants were recruited to contract for the sale of opium to registered smokers within a limited time. Simultaneously, the public Shanghai Hospital and Shanghai Charity Hospital were entrusted to handle smoking cessation experiments. All smokers who voluntarily confessed to drug use or applied for smoking cessation could be sent to the hospitals for free treatment. The details are as follows:

Smoker Registration: The public security organs, district offices, and social education organs advised and encouraged people to register in accordance with the regulations based on the survey results, or to voluntarily quit smoking. At the same time, the public security bureaus and offices were urged to conduct a thorough investigation to ensure that no smoker in the county was missed. However, smokers were deeply addicted and often waited and evaded registration. Therefore, starting in mid-August, the public security organs were forced to proceed. By the end of September, a total of 1,305 smokers had registered in the county.

Opium Sales and Smoking: After recruiting merchants to contract for opium shops and smoking dens, many applied to contract for opium shops and smoking dens. Subsequently, the Anti-Smoking Committee resolved that each self-governing district should have one opium shop, and each market town could have one or two smoking dens. At the same time, the Anti-Smoking Committee verified whether the guarantors of each applicant were reliable and whether the procedures were complete, and submitted them to the Anti-Smoking Committee for approval in order of application before transferring them for the issuance of licenses. The applications of the following opium shops have now been approved and reported: Minhang in the first district, Tangwan in the second district, Maqiao in the third district, Sanlin in the fourth district, and Chenhang in the fifth district. The approved smoking dens include two in Minhang, two in Maqiao, two in Beiqiao, two in Zhuanqiao, two in Tangwan, two in Caohang, two in Sanlin, one in Chenhang, one in Tiqiao, one in Tangkou, and one in Hehua, for a total of 18.

Persuasion to Quit Smoking: When registering smokers, smokers in various places were also persuaded to voluntarily confess and quit. As there was no smoking cessation center at that time, the committee negotiated with the public Shanghai Hospital to handle the matter on its behalf. The committee provided the costs of meals and medicine. Later, as the hospital's fourth-class wards were limited and the capacity for smokers was limited, the committee negotiated with the Shanghai Charity Hospital to handle the matter on its behalf. As of September, a total of 91 smokers had quit at the two hospitals. 111 people had registered for proxy rehabilitation. Including licensed smokers, the total number of smokers in the county was 1,507, accounting for 1.3% of the county's total population.

Establishment of a Smoking Cessation Center: In late August, the provincial government ordered the establishment of a smoking cessation center before September 30. The committee immediately prepared to rent a civilian house in Qiaojiazhai near the county seat as the site. While hiring workers to repair it, the committee selected Dr. Yu Jufang as the smoking cessation director and appointed him as the preparatory director in advance (to actively carry out the work). The house repairs have now been completed, and all necessary items have been purchased with county funds. It was formally established on October 1. In the early stages, the county issued notices to the districts to send the registered smokers to the center for treatment. The county also posted notices throughout the county stating that all licensed smokers who were determined to quit smoking early could also apply for treatment at the center. Smokers only had to pay a meal fee of 10 cents per day, and no other fees were charged. If there were any adverse reactions to smoking cessation, they would be treated free of charge to show compassion. There are currently 40 smokers undergoing treatment at the center.

Establishment of a Clinic: County Magistrate Pan decided that since the new county seat did not have a hospital, the Anti-Smoking Committee would also set up a clinic to handle medical treatment and health and epidemic prevention matters. All consultations were undertaken voluntarily by Dr. Yu and others, and no consultation or health fees were charged. Medicines were also given free of charge to the poor and sick, which was very well received locally.

Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance Changes the Tax Rate on Flat Box Matches 132

To be changed to Class B Consolidated Tax from this month.

Request for exemption of consolidated tax on matches in Fujian Province is denied.

The Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance believes that the total tax on matches should be changed as soon as possible. Yesterday, it specially changed the flat box matches to Class B consolidated tax. The request of match merchants for exemption of the consolidated tax on matches in Fujian Province in order to restore the original market has been rejected. The details are as follows:

Consolidated Tax on Matches: According to Chief Fang of the Match Section of the Tax Department yesterday:

Change in Tax Rate: A reporter from the Ta Kung News Agency reported that the tax rate on flat box matches levied by the Tax Department was originally collected according to Class A, at 13.40 yuan per box. However, as the length of the match happens to meet the conditions for paying Class B match tax, all match manufacturers across the country have been notified to change to Class B tax rate from the 1st of this month. The actual tax collected is 17.50 yuan per box. Match manufacturers have expressed their willingness to accept it, and there are no obstacles in the future.

Fujian Tax Exemption: As for the National Match Industry Federation, Fujian Province's

Reply Denied: The Tax Department has been informed that tax-evading matches from Japan are becoming more and more prevalent, and domestic matches have no room to stand. It has requested that the tax payable on domestic matches in Fujian Province be exempted from entry. The Tax Department believes that this concerns national tax revenue and the Ministry of Finance cannot rashly abandon it. Moreover, since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, there has been no precedent for temporarily exempting the consolidated tax that has already been implemented. Therefore, the request has been rejected.

The Taxpayers' Association Requests Compensation for Victims of Public Bus Accidents 134

The Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association received a petition from Zhang Yaoting yesterday, and forwarded a letter to John Thorburn, General Manager of the Public Concession Works Department, requesting that the company be ordered to provide generous compensation using legally legitimate administrative procedures for those injured by public bus accidents. The respective letters are recorded as follows:

Zhang Yaoting's Petition 135

Petitioner Zhang Yaoting, 47 years old, resident of 3345 Robert Road, Shanghai West, is submitting this petition because of a tragic accident, and humbly requests your assistance and to seek legal compensation. The petitioner's son, Hua Wen, was intelligent and had studied at the high school department of Shanghai Private Middle School. The principal, Chen Jicheng, praised his character and learning and gave him special treatment by providing free tuition. However, due to extreme poverty in the family, on August 16th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, he applied for a job at the Kang Nao Tuo Road Public Bus Company and was hired as a ticket seller with a monthly salary of 23 yuan, which was enough to feed the entire family. He also set up a Shaw English Night School at home as a side business. Tragically, on November 23rd of the same year, after 1:00 PM, while going to the company to submit his ticket stubs, he was hit and killed by the company's No. 15039 Route 2 bus near Sichuan Road and Aido Ya Road. Regarding the negligent driver Zhao Zhongran, the petitioner received a judgment from the Supreme Court on the 17th of this month (September), which upheld the original judgment, sentencing the defendant Zhao Zhongran to a fine of 200 yuan for the crime of causing death due to negligence in his duties, and the attached private lawsuit for 10,764 yuan has been transferred to the civil court by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court for filing. However, the right to adjudicate the company lies with the consul of the country stationed in Shanghai, and the petitioner finds it difficult to sue. The petitioner has only this one son, on whom he depends for his livelihood, and the entire family of four depends on his support. He died suddenly while serving the company, and he was killed by the company's bus. Under the circumstances, the company should provide generous compensation so that the living can be supported and the dead can be buried, which is in accordance with human sentiment. Moreover, according to Article 188 of the Civil Code, which stipulates that if an employer unlawfully infringes on the rights of others in the performance of his duties, the employer and the actor shall be jointly and severally liable for compensation for damages. In terms of legal principles, the company shall not evade its liability for compensation for damages. However, the company completely ignores the pain of the deceased and the bereaved family, treats human life as worthless, and turns a blind eye. Since Hua's death, the petitioner has lost his support and has no way to make a living. The entire family is old and weak and is in danger of freezing and starvation. The tragic situation is very alarming, and everyone who sees it sighs and feels injustice. I humbly ask your association, which has always been concerned about the people's suffering and is admired by Chinese and foreigners, to support the weak and suppress the strong, and is relied on by the wronged and the miserable. The petitioner is extremely wronged and is in extreme difficulty. I hope that you will have compassion and grant your assistance. In particular, I petition your association to humbly request that the Kang Nao Tuo Road Bus Company be immediately instructed to compensate the amount of 10,764 yuan for the attached private lawsuit, calculated from the dead person's monthly salary of 23 yuan while serving in the company, from the age of 21 to the age of 60. I also beg you to send a letter to the consulate, instructing them to remit the full amount of compensation so that both the living and the dead can be at peace. I respectfully submit this to the Shanghai Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association.

Letter to the Works Department 136

Dear Sir, we have received a document from Zhang Yaoting stating that his son, Zhang Huawen, was killed by a bus of the Public Concession Bus Company. After final trial by the court, the driver, Zhao Zhongran, was found guilty of causing death due to negligence in his duties and was fined 200 yuan, etc. It has come to the attention of the association that public buses have repeatedly caused major accidents, resulting in death or injury, but have never provided compensation or assumed responsibility. This is due to your department's failure to supervise and manage them, and especially to your negligence in strictly enforcing the issuance of driver's licenses. This association believes that your department is responsible for all accidents caused by public buses, which has emboldened the company to dare not take responsibility. The matter concerns public utilities. We are sending you a copy of the original document for your review, and request that you quickly use legally legitimate administrative procedures to order the company to provide generous compensation to show its responsibility. Sincerely, to the General Manager of the Shanghai Public Concession Works Department.

Reply to Zhang Yaoting 137

Dear Mr. Zhang Yaoting, your letter of September 29 regarding the death of Zhang Huawen caused by the driver of a public bus, Zhao Zhongran, due to negligence in his duties has been received and noted. Although we have won this case in law, it is very difficult to enforce due to the obstruction of consular jurisdiction. This association is also in a position where we cannot help. However, as public buses are public utilities, the Public Concession Works Department is in a position to supervise and manage them. If the department can do its best to fulfill its responsibilities, it will not be difficult to obtain administrative and moral relief. We have now forwarded a letter to the department to handle the matter. This reply is for Mr. Zhang Yaoting.

This government has repeatedly received reports from various organs and letters and telegrams from the Shanghai Qidong Fellow-Citizens Association, stating that the Baohua steamer was driven carelessly, resulting in the drowning of many lives in the Sanhe Port on the 12th, requesting that it be detained for investigation. This government should accept the case.
