Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Japan's Second Step Policy 251

— Xing An

According to yesterday's newspaper report, on the third anniversary of the September 18th Incident, the Nagoya Shimbun in Japan published a commentary entitled "The Asian Continent Construction Project Has Entered the North China Work Period of the Second Step." This article discussed the past aggression against Korea and Manchuria, and the steps to annex our country in the future. The Japanese ambition is completely exposed.

The commentary begins by saying: "Today is the third anniversary of the Manchurian Incident. What we feel in our hearts is that Japan's mission for the Asian continent policy is permanent and significant." It continues: "As for the mission of the Asian continent, it is entirely tied to our Japanese people. Since the Manchurian Incident occurred, it has been the time to realize our mission." Although there are only a few words, the entire Japanese nation's conspiracy against us has been frankly publicized, which is enough to awaken the delusions of the people.

"The construction work of Manchuria is gradually becoming smooth. At the same time, Japan hopes that the political work in North China will also become more coordinated. That is, Japan has now taken another step and is standing in the period of political work in North China. In other words, we have encountered the period of the second continental construction project." This is another very straightforward expression. Here, he tells us that Japan's continental policy has not only achieved initial success, but has also entered the second stage. Regarding Japan's continental policy, it is impossible for outsiders to know how many stages they are divided into.

The article also says: "But the great mission that Japan bears on the Asian continent, although it has started with the creation of Manchuria, cannot be said to have fulfilled its responsibilities. We should take the entire China and the entire Asia as our goals, and strive for cultural and economic unity and harmony. From the cause of creating Manchuria, we will promote it to the mainland of China, so that it will have the same sympathy and feelings as the Japanese people and become an inseparable relationship. This is our greatest ideal for Manchuria." These sentences are written even more vividly. I wonder what the people of our country will think when they see them?

Moonlight Night 252

— TT

The night is deathly quiet.

The moon hangs high in the clear sky, sending intermittent firecracker sounds from afar, vaguely vibrating in my ears.

The desolation here is more like a ghost realm than the ruins after a war. Living in this ghost realm, I occupy a bean-sized area on the earth, but I dare not believe that I am still a member of the world, because everything here makes me doubt the existence of life.

I have been here for about two months. In these two months, except for necessary outings, I have been hiding in this broken and old hut all day long; either sleeping or sitting blankly. Sometimes I also fulfill my bad habit, and start pacing. While pacing, I recite a poem I have always liked by Huang Zhongze, "Nine out of ten people deserve a scornful look, a hundred useless things is a scholar." Tired, I fell back on the straw mat spread on the ground, my bed, closed my eyelids, and reality, disappeared in my dreams.

Tonight, the moon is exceptionally round, and a few more firecrackers can be heard from afar, I guess it is the Mid-Autumn Festival.

Every festival makes me miss my relatives even more, and haven’t I always been like this? Of course, in my actions this time, I have fully demonstrated that I am a heartless and unfeeling person, but for this, I don’t know how many tears I have shed secretly. It was not until the day I had to leave that I painfully left my old home.

Mentioning the day I left home, besides crying loudly, what other way can I save the pain in my heart?

A cold morning. The sun had just emerged from the mountain peak. Except for the little birds on the locust tree branches in front of the courtyard, singing their morning songs, the earth was so silent. The alarm clock on the desk woke me up. I got out of bed with sleepy eyes, stretched my neck and looked out the window. I was shocked. The color of the sky told me it was already late. I hurriedly put on my clothes, took a rattan bag, bid farewell to my bedroom, and walked straight to the outer room, but as soon as I stepped out of the door, my calves seemed to soften, and a burst of sadness and tears rolled down uncontrollably. I guessed that they had discovered my sudden departure from the family without telling them, and I wondered how sad they would be. The faces of my mother crying with swollen eyes, and my younger siblings shedding tears appeared immediately before my eyes, but for myself, I finally gritted my teeth, endured the piercing pain, and resolutely walked towards the pier by the river. From that day until now, I have cut off all contact with my family. Under the moonlight tonight, I wonder if my younger siblings who are eating mooncakes are still thinking about their missing brother?

Amateur Mailbox

It is Not Easy for Parents to Teach Their Children! 253

Editor:

I am an eighteen-year-old youth who has received higher education and now works in a bookstore. Life is not comfortable, but not very difficult either. Recently, I have been feeling a kind of distress due to conflicts in opinions within the family. Therefore, I am writing to you, sir, to ask you to help me resolve it.

The fact is this: I have parents, who are both around forty years old. I am their only son, so they love me very much. Their minds are not overly corrupt, but they are not new either; they are also extremely conservative. And since I am a young man, influenced by the environment, my thoughts are relatively radical, and I like movement and dislike stillness. Therefore, in our thoughts and actions, we have different opinions everywhere. I am also young and competitive, and often engage in great theoretical disputes when discussing a certain issue. Although the result is often that I yield and tolerate it, sometimes I have disregarded my parents’ advice and done things according to my own wishes. In this way, not only are they very angry, but I am also very painful. I often think this: I should be more patient with my parents, why bother arguing about reason? But whenever their thoughts and behaviors are incorrect (for example, they are very superstitious), I can't help but say a few words to persuade them and correct their mistakes. But as a result, they scold me instead, but their reasons are incorrect and without any basis.

Also, I like to talk with friends or participate in some gatherings among friends, but my parents always stop me, saying that I am wasting time and energy; and that in this era of declining morals and treacherous people, making friends is very dangerous; a careless influence from the outside world will lead to the path of depravity. But I know that my friends are very upright and honest. Not only is there no harm in them, but I can also get a lot of knowledge among those friends. Therefore, disputes often arise, and I am very distressed in spirit. Sir: If you ask me to submit to everything and completely follow my parents’ wishes, it seems too difficult to endure; but if I follow my own will and resist the family, I feel that it is wrong, and there is no need or reason to resist. How should I resolve this issue? Please give me a guide. I think there must be many young people in the world who are in the same situation as me. Sincerely, I wish you good health. Junyan

Editor's Note: What Junyan has raised is a common problem of family ideological conflict. On the parents’ side, they think they are very protective of their children, but because they cannot understand the nature of young people, they often excessively interfere in their children’s thoughts and actions because they love them too much, resulting in a kind of opposite result. The editor believes that this issue is a very important issue of family education and is worthy of open discussion. I hope that readers will speak out as much as possible on behalf of either the parents or the children.

Novel

Uncle's Braid (II)(I) 254

— Ling He

In the heart of the second master, he really felt that people like Fengyun were really nosy. Why bother worrying about other people's hair? In fact, he did not know that one day, everyone's braids would be cut off, because he knew that the change from autocracy to the Republic of China was an unstoppable thing, and he also agreed with the republican system. Since the Sino-Japanese War, China has been weak and unable to recover. Perhaps changing a political system will make it stronger. However, he was really reluctant to cut off a black and long braid, and obviously dragging it down would inevitably be ridiculed for not being civilized enough. Therefore, taking care of both sides, only hiding it under the hat was a way. However, his hard work was not easy to understand. Isn't that so? At this time, Brother Fengyun would also say:

"But I don't care about these. Let the Republic of China be good. As for the bird shit about braids, I don't want to hide it."

Brother Fengyun always spoke like this, and Zhizhai had no choice but to hum and hum, and then smile slightly.

Fengyun's profession was collecting cow dung. He didn't dare to delay any longer. He carried his dung basket and prepared to part ways with Zhizhai. The last sentence was:

"Okay, your brothers are from three factions. The eldest brother is a braid, the second brother is a braid on a plate, and the third brother is a monk." He laughed a few times and left. But after taking a few steps, he turned back and said:

"Brother Zhizhai, don't be angry. I'll keep you company. I have to go find cow dung."

Zhizhai watched him leave with a wry smile. He thought: There's really no way to deal with this kind of person.

Red Thread Steals the Box Opening Verse 257

The land is divided, each claiming kingship.

My heart is filled with worries, remember Xue Song.

He is stationed at the strategic city of Guo Zhou.

Tian Chengsi is close to the Qing, disregarding, intending to attack.

Rumors spread like startled cranes.

They all say feigning passage is secretly an attack.

Xue Song is anxious and helpless.

A female page suddenly appears.

Young, remembers treasure, a maiden.

It is Hongxian who is loyal to her lord.

Tonight she ventures alone into the tiger's den.

She will teach him to hold back his troops and seek peace.

She withdraws and dresses again.

Instantly, her hair is styled, her spirit like a rainbow.

With a sword at her waist, light as a swallow.

She leaps and her shadow vanishes.

The fortress is heavily guarded with flags.

In an instant, she has crossed countless barriers.

The lights are dim, the watch horns are silent.

The soldiers are half asleep.

Hongxian sneaks into the central tent like a snake or a heron.

She sees him leaning on a pillow, clothed, breathing heavily.

His eight-character birthdate is hidden in a golden box.

Hongxian takes it from beside his pillow and hides it in her bosom.

Before leaving, she places seven decapitated heads into his chest.

A warning, he dares not inspect the troops and show his strength again.

The thousand-mile journey home is not yet dawn.

She will calmly report her clever plan.

Frightened, he dares not cross the Leichi Lake east of the mountains.

You Lian (880)

Chen Lianqing, Qi Lianfang: *Little Golden Coin*, 5:00 PM to 6:00 PM

Crying Over Aloeswood Opening Verse 258

Golden wind and jade dew, a cool autumn breeze,

Sweet osmanthus blossoms in full bloom, fragrant.

All sounds are silent, the sky is still,

A full moon shines on the eastern wall.

A sentimental person is stifled before the window,

Thinking of my sister, my heart aches.

Remembering the deep affection we shared in the past,

How can one not feel sorrow?

Sister, I truly hoped to be with you forever,

To happily grow old together in a peaceful haven.

Unexpectedly, this change occurred halfway,

Scattering the loving mandarin ducks in sorrow.

I ordered the children to buy aloeswood,

To carve your beautiful face from when you were alive.

It is difficult to carve your bright and lively eyes,

Difficult to carve your chaste and graceful figure.

Difficult to carve you embroidering mandarin ducks under the window during the day,

Difficult to carve you sitting alone reading *Romance of the Western Chamber* by the lamp.

Difficult to carve us enjoying flowers and drinking fragrant wine together,

Difficult to carve us playing chess, each claiming victory.

Difficult to carve your virtuous and capable goodness,

Difficult to carve your gentle voice and fragrant breath.

Difficult to carve your captivating beauty,

Difficult to carve our intimate words in the boudoir.

Sister, now I don't think about food or drink all day,

In my lovesick dreams, I meet you in your finery.

My pillow is cold, my quilt empty, I cannot sleep,

Grieving the cold wind and rain.

Today is the Mid-Autumn Festival,

Red candles shine brightly, and incense is lit again.

I respectfully invite you, sister, to sit in the place of honor,

Your younger brother accompanies you by your side.

Several plates of fruits you loved when you were alive,

Mooncakes, shortbread, and more.

Pears and water chestnuts were your favorites,

A branch of tender reed, white as frost.

I offer a cup of fragrant tea with both hands,

Sister, please have some snacks and tea in my room.

Sister, when you had a minor illness,

I tirelessly sought doctors and medicine.

Unexpectedly, the illness was incurable,

Your beautiful face and jade bones buried in the tomb.

Your last words still engraved in my heart,

I am filled with sorrow and tears.

You said that after you pass away,

I must diligently study under the window.

Make a name for yourself,

Marry a beautiful woman like a flower.

And keep you in my heart,

Sister, since you left this world,

My eyes are filled with tears all day long.

I have no heart to read or write,

Nor do I think of a wedding night.

After I complete three years of mourning,

I will shave my head and chant Buddhist scriptures.

So that we may be together again in the next life.

Lili (1240)

*Shen Bao* Local Supplement, Film Supplement

The Reputation of Stars Is the Prison of Stars (Part Two) 260

— Zhu Jia Bo

Jasu Pitts said: "Von Stroheim thought I could perform, but many people laughed when they saw me on the screen for the first time. That laughter built high walls around me, making it impossible for me to escape. From then on, I became a prisoner of all my facial and hand expressions. This was not only true in my career, but also in my private life, where I was subjected to an invisible restriction. I have never attended any banquets. In four years, I have never bought a dinner gown, because I already have a reputation for being 'ugly'. They don't invite me to banquets either. I also prefer to stay at home and play with the kids to avoid their harsh criticisms. Children don't criticize me harshly. They don't think I'm ugly, but think I'm beautiful. They never laugh at me, but laugh with me."

Greta Garbo is also a prisoner deeply confined in a mysterious jail. The walls created by her mysterious reputation are even stronger than ancient castles. If Garbo were to break free from her chains and try to escape from this prison, bugles would sound, guards would rise up, and she would be surrounded, making it impossible for her to escape. Therefore, she has to live in seclusion, not allowed to casually go to other studios besides her own to chat with other colleagues, not allowed to joke and laugh arbitrarily, and not allowed to stroll casually down the streets of Hollywood.

Irene Dunne said: "I am also a prisoner of professional thought or professional reputation. They all think I am a perfect woman, as if I would faint if I heard an immoral word, or cover my nose with a handkerchief when I encountered someone drinking. In fact, I often want to hear people's jokes and laugh heartily. I can also drink a cocktail in appropriate settings. But I am too burdened by this 'good reputation.'" The opposite of Irene Dunne's situation is Mae West, with her hourglass figure. Her good reputation is entirely that of a harlot, because she is good at playing lewd women on screen. Over time, her prison has been built and cannot be broken. In fact, West does not drink or smoke, nor does she attend night banquets. She is a proper housewife. Of course, she is definitely not like what you see on screen, often luring men to her home for a visit.

Perhaps the most severely imprisoned is Janet Gaynor. There is probably no chance for her to escape from her prison forever. Once, a female reporter visited Janet. At that time, Janet had just been married to Lydell Peck not long ago. She saw the reporter and said happily in the conversation that she really wanted to have a child. The reporter thought it was a very common thing, and every virtuous wife always wants to have a baby after marrying a man. Unexpectedly, after the reporter returned home, she received a call from the film company asking her not to publish Janet's words about having a child in the newspaper. The reporter said that it is a very common thing for women to have children, so why aren't they even allowed to publish that hope in the newspaper? But the people in the company said: "That's not allowed. If you publish those words, her reputation will be ruined. She will always be a little girl. She is youth. She is sweetness. She is glory. She must not come into contact with everything in life. The matter of having children is especially out of the question!" Recently, rumors have been spreading that Janet suddenly had an affair with a married man. Everyone is whispering in panic, as if Hollywood would collapse if that were confirmed.

Slice White once said sadly: "I am a prisoner, probably a prisoner for life! I am forever imprisoned under the infamous name of 'gold digger', and I cannot break free. It's really strange. But I am a good housekeeper, and I recently demonstrated my cooking skills in front of five hundred women. I can knit Afghan sweaters. I can make Italian noodles. I can steam cocoa cakes better than anyone else. I know how to save money. I arrive at the studio on time and am never late. I also don't have any dealings with male colleagues. But, in the eyes of people in the world, I am still a dazzling and unattainable blonde dangerous woman."

The above are all common prisoners. Valentino became an Aheilr for life. Irene Dunne is an eternally perfect woman. Janet Gaynor is a little sister who will never grow up. Mae West is an incorrigible siren. Slice White is a woman who values money and not reputation. Garbo is always a solitary walker. Each of them is individually imprisoned in a room, isolated, so that their characteristics will never be mixed and adulterated! (The End)

Film Review

Review of *The Line Up* 261

— Ling He

The Line Up - Cathay

From all aspects, we cannot give this film a higher evaluation, because it is just a mediocre detective film.

However, the theme adopted here is relatively fresh. The playwright placed a group of clothes-stealing thieves, along with a woman, and this woman fell in love with a detective. As a result, the gang of thieves was solved, and the woman and the detective went on a sweet trip. The mediocrity of the story can be seen from this.

The director's technique has a fairly bright tone and progresses smoothly. Especially the last part, when the two detectives searched the clothing store and had not yet discovered the secret organization, due to appropriate editing, the tense and funny atmosphere was indeed very good.

The acting skills of the actors, when reviewed individually, have no special merits, but several of the main ones can still develop evenly, at least they can perform the mediocre play in a mediocre way.

That's how it is, the ultimate mediocrity, nothing more.

Film Notes 262

— Yin Shi

1. Several types of films that China lacks.

Obviously: Since the "September 18th Incident" and the "January 28th Incident," the two extraordinary events, Chinese films have made very obvious progress due to the rise of national consciousness and the awakening of the film industry itself. At least - those films with gods, monsters, martial arts that are harmful to national thought have disappeared from the film scene.

However, although current Chinese films have made significant progress, they still lack several types of films in terms of quality, such as social education films, children's education films, science films, physiology films, and films that use war as a background to instill military knowledge to the public... Undoubtedly, the above types of films are currently very much needed, but we have not yet heard of a company that will produce the above films. This is truly a very regrettable thing!

2. Hope the Film Association can be realized soon

Recently, there has been such a rumor in the film industry that eight companies, including so-and-so, intend to organize a film trade association, stipulating that a group meeting will be held once or twice a month to jointly discuss the steps for the progress of film art, and on the other hand, it can also explain the misunderstandings between companies. Indeed: At a time when companies are mutually hostile, fighting each other internally, and the foreign film industry is stepping up its aggression against the Chinese film front, the establishment of a film trade association is most urgently needed.

3. The Physical Health of Stars

The poor physical health of Chinese film stars (including male and female stars) is indeed an undeniable fact, except for a few who are willing to exercise.

We know that with a healthy body, we can have a sound career, and working in films is more likely to damage the body than other jobs. The separation of day and night, the disharmony of hot and cold, and the endless working hours, if you do not have a healthy body to resist, eventually your body will become weaker and more ill. Your great future will be buried in a weak and sickly body.

Chinese film stars, I hope you will not be obsessed with those handball courts or dance halls that are harmful to money and body after work. You should use this spare time to work hard to exercise and enrich your physical health. Look! The reason why every star in Hollywood is so healthy is the reward they get for being willing to exercise!

Datong Company Comes to Shanghai to Shoot Interior Scenes 263

— Bo Zhong

Wan Laitian, who once served as director of Mingxing, Shenzhou, Great China, Minxin, and Lianhua companies, has been working hard in Sichuan for film culture movement with his friend Zhao Chuan since directing the film "Heartache." Because of the barriers of mountains and rivers, news is not communicated, so for two or three years, the news has been silent.

Currently, Wan has founded a film school and a drama troupe in Sichuan. The film school has more than 400 students. Recently, Wan and Ms. Huang Hou organized Datong Film Company, and the debut work is "Under Mount Emei." The purpose of the play is to expose the dark side of politics in Sichuan. The subject matter is extremely realistic and touching. The exterior scenes have been filmed in Sichuan, and the interior scenes are inconvenient due to material aspects, so they came to Shanghai to shoot them the day before yesterday. The female lead is Ms. Huang Hou. Huang is a graduate of Shanghai Tsinghua Art College and has profound attainments in film and drama.

Before entering the film industry, Lu was a dance professor at the Jimei Dance Troupe. She has a very deep understanding of singing, so the results are extremely beautiful.

The song has been published in the New Garden on the 3rd of this month. The author is Gao Tianqi, and the singer is the heroine Miss Fan Xuepeng.

"Film Stories" Published 266

The "Film Stories" compiled by Xie Jun'en and published by Liangyou Publishing Company has been published. It contains more than 400,000 words, including nearly 400 stories of foreign films released in China in the past ten years. They are divided into history, society, religion, ethics, love, tragedy, chivalry, war, detective, adventure, aviation, science, etc. The outline is comprehensive and extremely perfect. There is also an English index directory, which is especially convenient for checking. With a copy in hand, it will surely be a must-have for film lovers. This is specially written as an introduction. The Editors of this publication

Brief Guidelines for Submitting to the *Shen Bao* Film Supplement 267

1. This publication is a film publication that assists cultural promotion and artistic expression. We welcome external submissions and will provide generous compensation upon publication.

2. Once the text is published and compensated, the copyright belongs to *Shen Bao*.

3. The text of this publication is mainly in vernacular Chinese and must use modern punctuation.

4. If the submission is a translation, the original work should be attached, and English should be omitted if possible.

5. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper or write horizontally, and do not use a pencil.

6. If multiple submissions of one manuscript, plagiarism, or reproduction of text or explanatory materials are discovered, no compensation will be given.

Film Novels

Long Live Freedom (Viva Villa) (6) 268

— Wen Ying

Fero heard Sykes' words and, believing them to be true, took him to find Banjo. Sykes entered the station and suddenly wanted to send a telegram to the New York newspaper, so he discussed it with Fero, waiting for them in the telegraph room, and told the other two robbers to go and find Banjo. Here, Sykes moved a typewriter from the ground, inserted a piece of paper, and started typing a news report, reporting the true situation of Banjo and his gang of robbers retaking Laconsi Boarding. At this time, Banjo and his subordinates Thomas and Waltis were in a looted shop. They had captured seven women there, and Banjo was inspecting them one by one. He looked at them with a playful smile, and they all wanted to please Banjo, letting him flirt with them. However, when Banjo flirted with the fifth woman, the woman showed a disgusted look. Banjo asked her what her name was. She said her name was Lucinda. Banjo said, "What's the matter? Are you afraid of me? You don't need to be afraid. I am very loyal." As he spoke, he reached out to pinch her fair face. Unexpectedly, the woman became enraged and slapped Banjo in the face. Banjo shouted, "Oh, good, Thomas, I want this one. Lucinda, come with me. Don't you want to provoke me?" He pulled her hand hard and hugged her. Lucinda kept slapping him in the face. Thomas came over and gently picked her up. Lucinda shouted, "If you want me, you should marry me. I won't go with a thief!" At this moment, Waltis walked up to Banjo and reported that Fero was looking for him, and someone wanted to see him in the telegraph room at the station. Banjo ordered Waltis to help Thomas. Lucinda kept shouting at Banjo, "If you want me, you must marry me!" Banjo turned around and scolded, "Bullshit!" and walked away.

Banjo walked into the telegraph room, and Fero nodded at Sykes, who was typing. Banjo walked behind Sykes, watching him type. At this time, the paper read: "Laconsi Boarding, Mexico, August 15th. The bandit army, led by the outlaw Banjo Villa, suddenly invaded this place today. After the bandits arrived, they burned and looted everywhere, and the entire territory was looted. The atrocities of rape and murder are unspeakable..." Sykes was typing when he suddenly looked up and saw a bloated and clumsy ugly man, and asked, "Are you Banjo Villa?" Banjo Villa said, "Yes." Sykes quickly covered the paper on the typewriter and shouted, "Don't look, don't look. I have to rewrite it." Banjo stretched out a thick and fat finger and pointed to a word on the paper, "Is this my name? Hmm, my name, Banjo Villa? What else does it say?" Sykes heard this and breathed a sigh of relief, saying, "What? Can't you read? What it says above is probably reporting how your brave brothers overcame the central army, as well as your personal genius, etc." Banjo said, "Is this what you wrote to America?" Sykes said, "Of course, six million people can't eat breakfast every morning without reading my news." Banjo scratched his head and said, "This is too short. Can't you write more?" Sykes was happy to hear this and said, "Oh, if you can find a way to get your brothers to take a walk outside, my mind can work more peacefully." Banjo heard this and immediately ordered everyone to go outside. Sykes said again, "I can't write well without wine. That person robbed my wine." Banjo immediately snatched the bottle of wine back and gave it to Sykes, then said, "You tell the Americans that Banjo Villa is not afraid of death." (To be continued)
